                    One Write, All. One person writes the entire document. Team
                    gives feedback. Consistent style but unfair workload. Works
                    well for short documents.

                    style, but can be tedious, frustrating, and Inefficient. May
                    work reasonably well for very short documents.
                    Each Writes Part. Team member1 divide and delegate the
                    writing and share in giving feedback. Time efficient and equi•
                    table workloads, but inconsistent writing style. Works well for
                    long documenb. Delays can <Xcur when deadlines aren 1t met.
